 He said that all the biometric data of Aadhaar is protected with 2048 bit encryption
 yah desi takanic he
 We have just licensed the technology of biometric data matching from the world's best known company
 haalanki is takanic kaa istemaal hamaare apane sarwar se hota he
 Pandey said that in the last 15 years the exercise of Aadhaar has reached from thought to behavior
 No National ID se Online ID tak ke safar ke is tarah ke abhyaas kaa prayaas insaan dwaara kahin bhi nahin kiya gaya he
 It is so secure that breaking an encryption will take time equal to the age of the universe
 yah takanic behad unnat bhi he or sasti bhi
 He said that the cost of an Aadhaar card is less than a dollar
 aadhaar project par sarkaar ne ab tak nau hajaar karod rupee kharch kiye hai
 The allegations of Aadhaar data leaks are baseless
 yah sach he ki biometric software baahar se mangaya gaya he, lekin data control hamaare paas he
 Aadhaar's 6000 servers are not connected to the Internet

 Personal information is provided for KYC only
